 1883 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      5 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0C83               | * Compiles shape data into native 65816 code that
 1884 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      6 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0C83               | * draws sprites via direct-page writes to SHR shadow RAM.
 1885 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      7 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0C83               | *
 1886 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      8 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0C83               | * Call: copy sprite table ($18 bytes) to bank $00 direct page,
 1887 |  2 Create.Sprite.s      9 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0C83               | *       LDA #dp_address / JSR Create_Sprite
 1888 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     10 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0C83               | *
 1889 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     11 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0C83               | * Sprite table format (24 bytes at DP offsets $00-$17):
 1890 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     12 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0C83               | *   $00 ADRL Rout_Adr    — output: where compiled code is written

 1892 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     14 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0C83               | *   $08 ADRL Msk_Adr     — $000000=none, $FFFF00=auto, $FEFE00=decor

 1894 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     16 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0C83               | *   $0E DA   Nb_Lgn      — bytes per shape row
 1895 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     17 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0C83               | *   $10 DA   Nb_Col      — bytes per shape column
 1896 |  2 Create.Sprite.s     18 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0C83               | *   $12 DA   Lgn         — row ($FFFF=dynamic via Y register)
